data-review-title-typography="true"><h2 class="typography_heading-xs__osRhC typography_appearance-default__t8iAq" data-service-review-title-typography="true">Awful for Teachers, Useless for Students, Suspicious Reviews</h2></a><p class="typography_body-l__v5JLj typography_appearance-default__t8iAq" data-service-review-text-typography="true">What happened to the 3.0 rating that Twenix previously had? Like magic, it has changed. If you see any positive ratings from &quot;tweachers&quot; about this company, notice that they all only have 1 review so Twenix is likely fabricating their ratings or incentivizing teachers to write these reviews that sound like they are straight out of ChatGPT. Twenix will automatically terminate your teaching account if your feedback score sits below 4.7. The algorithm they use is flawed because I began receiving automated emails and warnings about poor performance the same week I onboarded before even completing a week of teaching. On top of that, teachers are not rated based on how well they cover the terrible course material, but instead on how entertaining they are. If you are a student/company using Twenix for your learning, you are wasting your time and money. Where Twenix really shines is  making ignorant students feel like they are making progress or truly developing their skills, when they are in fact, just wasting their time and money and supporting a company that exploits teachers. From onboarding to termination, you will never see anyone from the company on camera or ever be given anyone&#x27;s real name. How companies like this can exist within the EU is astonishing.<br/><br/>UPDATE: In response to Twenix&#x27;s reply on 6/4/24.<br/><br/>Yes, there are other negative reviews for other companies similar to Twenix that operate on similar exploitative business models. As teachers, we need to continue to hold these companies accountable and make it clear to students what exactly they are supporting by using these companies.<br/><br/>Of course, reviews fluctuate. The suspicion comes from the number of positive reviewers (especially from South Africa) who have no other reviews on Trustpilot.<br/><br/>In regards to the rating system, you can find the same problem reported by other past employees across Glassdoor, Google Reviews, as well as other critical reviews posted here on Trustpilot. <br/><br/>As for the lack of a &quot;personal touch&quot;, as you put it. I will reiterate that from onboarding to termination, the whole process was automated. </p><p class="typography_body-m__k2UI7 typography_appearance-default__t8iAq" Ratings are reviewed weekly, and warnings are only issued after multiple weeks of similar rating issues or absences.<br/><br/>Additionally, Twenix staff members often sign emails with their real names, and we conduct webinars twice a week led by our team on camera.
